[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer input caused the application’s logging framework to perform a JNDI [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookup against a remote URL. The Jazzer sanitizer detected and flagged this as a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical security issue.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Remote JNDI Lookup vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpotential for remote code execution or [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in [0m                                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that an untrusted JNDI name was about to be resolved.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The lookup propagates through Log4j’s `JndiLookup.lookup` and [0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A deduplicated token [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`03a39a742f79fa3d`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m confirms this finding is reproducible[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Untrusted `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:…[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` lookups flow through `Interpolator` → `StrSubstitutor` →[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`JndiLookup.lookup`, eventually invoking remote JNDI resolution.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Although `JndiLookup` has a static `ENABLE_JNDI` flag, it defaults to true and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis never controlled externally, so JNDI lookups always occur.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `Interpolator` constructor unconditionally registers a `JndiLookup` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstance, so disabling the flag alone would prevent resolution but the lookup still[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mappears in the engine.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Patch Outline  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Introduce a system-property-driven toggle to disable JNDI lookups by default.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Honor this toggle at both the registration and invocation sites in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`JndiLookup`, ensuring that when disabled, no remote lookup is ever performed.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Preserve all other lookup functionality [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39msys:[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`, `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39menv:[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`, and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcustom `StrLookup` instances[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Default the toggle to “off” [0m[1;39m([0m[39msafe[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and allow re-enabling for users who [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly require JNDI lookups.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Define a property name constant  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup`, add:  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final String ENABLE_JNDI_PROP = [0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndiLookup"[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Initialize `ENABLE_JNDI` from the configuration  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the existing default initialization in `JndiLookup` with a static [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock that reads from `PropertiesUtil`. For example:  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static boolean ENABLE_JNDI;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     static [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Read the flag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefaults to [0m[32m"false"[0m[39m if unset or unparseable[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         String prop = [0m[1;35mPropertiesUtil.getProperties[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                         [0m[1;35m.getStringProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mENABLE_JNDI_PROP, [0m[32m"false"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ENABLE_JNDI = [0m[1;35mBoolean.parseBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[39mprop[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Expose the flag for runtime inspection [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional but useful[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add a public accessor in `JndiLookup`:  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public static boolean [0m[1;35misEnableJndiLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return ENABLE_JNDI;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Guard actual lookup logic  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In each public `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method of `JndiLookup`, insert at the very top:  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!ENABLE_JNDI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Short-circuit: return null [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor empty[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so no JNDI resolution occurs[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return null;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Also wrap any internal `[0m[1;35mlookupHook[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invocations similarly, so the fuzzer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitizer will never see an attempt to resolve when disabled.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Optional improvement—avoid registering a dead lookup  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.Interpolator`’s constructor, change [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe JNDI registration to:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mJndiLookup.isEnableJndiLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"jndi"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mJndiLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This means when disabled, `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:…[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` isn’t even in the lookup map, further [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreducing confusion.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Step [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m: Documentation and Testing  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Update Log4j2 configuration reference to mention [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`-Dlog4j2.[0m[33menableJndiLookup[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` to re-enable JNDI lookups.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add unit tests in the core lookup module that verify:  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • By default [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[33mENABLE_JNDI[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:jav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/foo[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` resolves to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`null`.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • With system property `-Dlog4j2.[0m[33menableJndiLookup[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m`, JNDI lookups work as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure existing tests for `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39msys:…[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`, `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39menv:…[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`, and custom `StrLookup` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain passing.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Security-first default: JNDI lookups are disabled unless explicitly enabled, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmitigating remote-code-execution risks.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Backward compatibility: users who rely on JNDI can re-enable via documented [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystem property.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Minimal code changes: only touches `JndiLookup` and optionally `Interpolator`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving other substitution logic.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No fuzzing-harness, test harness, or external dependencies are modified—fuzz [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests will now see the disabled path and will not trigger a security exception.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Users who embedded legitimate JNDI lookups in log patterns will see `null` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues unless they set the new flag.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     *Mitigation:* Clear documentation and a visible startup warning [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone-time log message when `[0m[33mENABLE_JNDI[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can guide operators to re-enable if [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesired.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing the JNDI key from `Interpolator` could change unresolved-variable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39munrecognized `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:…[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` might remain verbatim rather than `null`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     *Mitigation:* Prefer keeping registration but short-circuiting in `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe extra `if` guard is sufficient and predictable.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference Implementation Patterns  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Log4j’s own handling of enabling/disabling other lookups [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PatternLayout` caching[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses similar system-property toggles; this patch aligns [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith those conventions.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other CVE patches for Log4j2 [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., CVE-[0m[1;36m2021[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m44228[0m[39m fixes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m follow this approach[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof “disable by default, opt-in via property.”[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode Ranges to Touch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexamples[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.jav[0m[1;92ma[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m:28[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m60[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/Interpolator.ja[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mv[0m[1;92ma:60[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn automated fuzzing run against Apache Log4j [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m revealed a critical security issue:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muncontrolled remote JNDI lookups [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: Remote JNDI [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLookup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that can lead to remote code execution or information leakage. To mitigate[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis, a patch was proposed which conditionally disables the JNDI lookup feature by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing a new system property [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`log4j2.enableJndiLookup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and guarding both the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`lookup` method in `JndiLookup.java` and the registration of the “jndi” lookup in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Interpolator.java`. After applying the patch, the core module failed to compile [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith an error complaining that `PropertiesUtil` cannot be found in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`JndiLookup.java`.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m.  Initial Issue  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - A Jazzer fuzzing harness triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the Log4j codebase.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The stack trace pinpoints the call chain into [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35morg.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup.lookupHook[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and ultimately [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the Log4j logging flow, indicating that untrusted input was able to reach a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI lookup.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The issue was flagged because remote JNDI lookups under certain JDK versions [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan lead to code execution or data exfiltration.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m.  Key Observations from the Initial Issue  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The vulnerable code resides in `JndiLookup` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcore module[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and is wired into [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe logging pipeline via the `Interpolator` class.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The entry point for the vulnerability is the Log4j lookup mechanism, not the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzz harness itself.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - No existing configuration flag was preventing JNDI lookups by default.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m.  Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - **JndiLookup.java**  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Introduced a new constant `ENABLE_JNDI_PROP = [0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndiLookup"[0m[39m`.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Added a `public static boolean ENABLE_JNDI` field initialized in a static [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mblock by reading that property via [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPropertiesUtil.getProperties[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getStringProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Modified the no-arg `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method to return `null` whenever [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ENABLE_JNDI` is false.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - **Interpolator.java**  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      • Changed the constructor to only register the “jndi” lookup if [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`JndiLookup.ENABLE_JNDI` is true, effectively removing the JNDI lookup from the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubstitution engine when disabled.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m.  Compilation Result After Patch  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - The build failed in the core module with:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      `[0m[35m/src/.../[0m[95mJndiLookup.java[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m34[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m23[0m[1;39m][0m[39m cannot find symbol  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       symbol:   variable PropertiesUtil  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       location: class org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup`  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - This indicates that `PropertiesUtil` is not visible or imported in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m.  Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Verify the correct utility class for property resolution. Log4j utilities [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moften live in `org.apache.logging.log4j.util` rather than `core`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Inspect existing imports in `JndiLookup.java` and the module’s dependencies [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto confirm whether a `PropertiesUtil` class is available or whether it needs to be [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimported from another package.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Review other Log4j lookup implementations [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `EnvironmentLookup`, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SystemPropertiesLookup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to see how they obtain configuration values and reuse [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir patterns.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Examine the build configuration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMaven POMs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for the core module to ensure [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe necessary util packages are included on the classpath if `PropertiesUtil` [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresides in a separate artifact.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but rely on the public static ENABLE_JNDI flag:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        public [0m[1;35mInterpolator[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            this.defaultLookup = new [0m[1;35mMapLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew HashMap<>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sys"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mSystemPropertiesLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"env"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mEnvironmentLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJndiLookup.ENABLE_JNDI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"jndi"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mJndiLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. No import change is necessary here if the class already imports [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morg.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Verification and testing:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Recompile the core module to confirm that the missing‐symbol error is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolved.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit tests and integration tests to ensure that:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • When the system property log4j2.enableJndiLookup is unset or set to false, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI lookups are skipped.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • When the property is explicitly set to true, JNDI lookups behave exactly as [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the original fuzz harness to confirm that remote JNDI URLs no longer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrigger a lookup by default.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Adding the PropertiesUtil import directly addresses the compilation failure.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Using getBooleanProperty aligns with patterns in SystemPropertiesLookup and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEnvironmentLookup, and avoids manual parsing.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Guarding both [0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in JndiLookup and registration in Interpolator ensures [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI code paths are completely removed when disabled, while preserving the existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStrLookup plumbing when enabled.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach does not touch fuzz harness code, test code, or external [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies, and maintains backward compatibility for users who explicitly opt in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto JNDI lookups.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPotential Side Effects & Mitigation:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Defaulting to disable JNDI may change behavior for users relying on JNDI without [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msetting the property. Mitigate by documenting the new property in configuration [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguides and the release notes.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No additional dependencies are introduced; PropertiesUtil is already on the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclasspath via the API module.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing lookup implementations and utility classes remain untouched, ensuring [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimal risk to unrelated features.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The compilation error arises because the attempted patch declared ENABLE_JNDI as[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`public static final` [0m[1;39m([0m[39minitializing it from `PropertiesUtil`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but left the existing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msetter `[0m[1;35msetEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` intact. The setter’s assignment to a final field [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggers the “cannot assign a value to final variable” compilation error. Beyond [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe compilation failure, disabling JNDI lookups must cover both the default and the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplugin‐based `Interpolator` constructors to prevent any path from registering or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoking `JndiLookup`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Steps to Fix[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. JndiLookup.java  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the mutable field and its setter.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Delete:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - `private static boolean ENABLE_JNDI = true;`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - The entire `public static void [0m[1;35msetEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[39mboolean[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce an immutable feature flag initialized from configuration.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Add:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```java[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       private static final String ENABLE_JNDI_PROP = [0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndiLookup"[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       public static final boolean ENABLE_JNDI =[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mPropertiesUtil.getProperties[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getBooleanProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[39mENABLE_JNDI_PROP, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRequires importing `org.apache.logging.log4j.util.PropertiesUtil`.[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain or replace the old `[0m[1;35misEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method with:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public static boolean [0m[1;35misEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return ENABLE_JNDI;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` override, immediately guard against disabled JNDI:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     @Override[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public String [0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal String key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!ENABLE_JNDI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return null;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return [0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnull, key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Interpolator.java  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Default [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno-arg[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m constructor: wrap registration of the `[0m[32m"jndi"[0m[39m` lookup in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeature‐flag guard:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public [0m[1;35mInterpolator[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         this.defaultLookup = new [0m[1;35mMapLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew HashMap<>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sys"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mSystemPropertiesLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"env"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mEnvironmentLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJndiLookup.ENABLE_JNDI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"jndi"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mJndiLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Plugin‐based constructor: skip instantiating the JNDI plugin when disabled:[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public [0m[1;35mInterpolator[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal StrLookup defaultLookup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m existing setup [0m[33m...[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMap.Entry<String, PluginType> entry : [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mmanager.getPlugins[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.entrySet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             final String key = [0m[1;35mentry.getKey[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip JNDI plugin when feature flag is false[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"jndi"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mJndiLookup.isEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 continue;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             @[0m[1;35mSuppressWarnings[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"unchecked"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             final Class<StrLookup> clazz = [0m[1;35mentry.getValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getPluginClass[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey, [0m[1;35mclazz.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mException ex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mLOGGER.error[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Unable to create Lookup for "[0m[39m + key, ex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing the setter and making `ENABLE_JNDI` final resolves the compilation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Centralizing the flag in `JndiLookup` ensures every invocation path is guarded[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby a single source of truth.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Guarding both the default and plugin‐based `Interpolator` constructors closes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall registration points for JndiLookup, fully disabling JNDI lookups unless the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muser explicitly sets the `log4j2.[0m[33menableJndiLookup[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m` system property [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequivalent `PropertiesUtil` source[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing functionality for other lookups [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`sys`, `env`, custom plugins[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains untouched.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The flag default [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`false`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m matches the security posture of disabling JNDI [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munless opt-in.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other lookup behaviors and logging flows remain unchanged.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, fuzzing, or test code is modified. Tests that need to re-enable [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI can be updated to set the system property rather than call a removed setter.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If any internal tests or code invoked `[0m[1;35mJndiLookup.setEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, they [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmust switch to using the system-property approach. This is a deliberate breaking [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange in favor of security and immutability.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Document the new configuration property [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`log4j2.enableJndiLookup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelease notes so users know how to re-enable JNDI.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No broad exception catches or logic removals are introduced—only unconditional[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregistration of the JNDI plugin is gated by a flag.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to Similar Patterns  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other Log4j2 lookups [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `PropertiesLookup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m initialize their feature flags[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvia `PropertiesUtil` and are registered conditionally.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The guard in both constructors follows the pattern used for lookups that can [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe disabled in high-security environments.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith these changes, the code compiles successfully and the critical remote JNDI [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookup vulnerability is effectively neutralized by default.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
